MPID_H_エルトシャン: Ruler of Nordion. Wields the Demon\nSword in knightly devotion to any master.\nOlder brother of Lachesis. Appears in\nFire Emblem: Genealogy of the Holy War.
MPID_H_クレイン: A young general of Etruria. Clarine's\nbrother. Treats all as equals. Appears in\nFire Emblem: The Binding Blade.
MPID_H_ラインハルト: Formidable and admired mage knight\nin Friege's army. Ever ready to lend\nan ear to his younger sister, Olwen.\nAppears in Fire Emblem: Thracia 776.
MPID_H_オルエン: A mage knight in Friege's army. Her\nideals sometimes put her in opposition\nwith her beloved brother, Reinhardt.\nAppears in Fire Emblem: Thracia 776.
MPID_H_ラケシス: Lady of House Nordion. Adores her older\nbrother, Eldigan, to the point that other\nmen pale in comparison. Appears in\nFire Emblem: Genealogy of the Holy War.
MPID_H_サナキ: Empress of Begnion. Known as\nthe Apostle, voice of the goddess.\nYoung but dutiful ruler. Appears in\nFire Emblem: Radiant Dawn.

MPID_H_ジャファル: An emotionless member of the Black Fang\nassassins. Known as the Angel of Death.\nAppears in Fire Emblem: The Blazing Blade.
MPID_H_カレル: A vicious swordsman from a family devoted to\nmastering the blade. Known as the Sword Demon.\nAppears in Fire Emblem: The Blazing Blade.
MPID_H_ニニアン: A young dancer who has a serene and mystical\npresence. Her dances are divine tributes.\nAppears in Fire Emblem: The Blazing Blade.
MPID_H_プリシラ: The daughter of Count Caerleon. Also Raven's\nsister. Poised and gentle, with a jealous streak.\nAppears in Fire Emblem: The Blazing Blade.
MPID_H_レベッカ: A girl who lives in a remote village and spends\nher time hunting. Kind and sociable. Appears\nin Fire Emblem: The Blazing Blade.
MPID_H_ルセア: A gentle cleric who serves Raven. Carries a\nheavy burden from a dark childhood. Appears\nin Fire Emblem: The Blazing Blade.

MPID_H_春祭カミラ: Princess of Nohr who dotes on her\nsibling Corrin. Loves her new outfit\never since Corrin said it was cute.\nAppears in Fire Emblem Fates.

MPID_H_水着ガイア: A thief from Ylisse known for his sweet\ntooth. Usually secrets candy in his clothes,\nbut can't when he's dressed like this.\nAppears in Fire Emblem Awakening.
MPID_H_水着フレデリク: A knight who serves the royal house of Ylisse.\nCollector of pebbles and shells on the beach.\nAppears in Fire Emblem Awakening.
MPID_H_水着ルフレ女: A tactician of Ylisse and Chrom's close ally. Loves\nthe strange creatures she finds on the beach.\nAppears in Fire Emblem Awakening.
MPID_H_水着チキ覚醒: Known as the Voice of the Divine Dragon. Has\nlived through thousands of summers, but usually\ndoesn't need to worry about swimming gear.\nAppears in Fire Emblem Awakening.

MSID_H_魚を突いた銛＋: At start of combat, if unit's HP = 100%, grants\nAtk/Spd/Def/Res+2, but after combat, if unit\nattacked, deals 2 damage to unit.

MSID_H_スイカ割りの棍棒＋: At start of combat, if unit's HP = 100%, grants\nAtk/Spd/Def/Res+2, but after combat, if unit\nattacked, deals 2 damage to unit.
MSID_H_氷菓子の弓: Effective against flying foes. At start of combat, if\nunit's HP = 100%, grants Atk/Spd/Def/Res+2, but\nafter combat, if unit attacked, deals 2 damage to\nunit.
MSID_H_氷菓子の弓＋: Effective against flying foes. At start of combat, if\nunit's HP = 100%, grants Atk/Spd/Def/Res+2, but\nafter combat, if unit attacked, deals 2 damage to\nunit.
MSID_H_貝殻: At start of combat, if unit's HP = 100%,\ngrants Atk/Spd/Def/Res+2, but after combat,\nif unit attacked, deals 2 damage to unit. After\ncombat, if unit attacked, inflicts Def/Res-5 on\nfoe through its next action.
MSID_H_貝殻＋: At start of combat, if unit's HP = 100%,\ngrants Atk/Spd/Def/Res+2, but after combat,\nif unit attacked, deals 2 damage to unit. After\ncombat, if unit attacked, inflicts Def/Res-7 on\nfoe through its next action.
MSID_H_HP守備1: Grants HP+3, Def+1.
MSID_H_HP守備2: Grants HP+4, Def+2.
MSID_H_近距離防御1: If foe initiates combat and uses sword, lance, axe,\nor dragonstone, grants Def/Res+2 during combat.
MSID_H_近距離防御2: If foe initiates combat and uses sword, lance, axe,\nor dragonstone, grants Def/Res+4 during combat.
MSID_H_近距離防御3: If foe initiates combat and uses sword, lance, axe,\nor dragonstone, grants Def/Res+6 during combat.
MSID_H_攻撃速さ封じ1: Inflicts Atk/Spd-3 on foe through its next action\nafter combat.
MSID_H_攻撃速さ封じ2: Inflicts Atk/Spd-5 on foe through its next action\nafter combat.
MSID_H_守備の謀策1: At start of turn, inflicts Def-3 on foes in cardinal\ndirections with Res < unit’s Res through their next\nactions.
MSID_H_守備の謀策2: At start of turn, inflicts Def-4 on foes in cardinal\ndirections with Res < unit’s Res through their next\nactions.
MSID_H_守備の謀策3: At start of turn, inflicts Def-5 on foes in cardinal\ndirections with Res < unit’s Res through their next\nactions.
MSID_H_槍の技量1: While unit lives and uses a lance, unit gets\n1.5x SP. (Only highest value applied. Does\nnot stack.)
MSID_H_槍の技量2: While unit lives, all lance allies on team get 1.5x\nSP. (Only highest value applied. Does not stack.)
MSID_H_槍の技量3: While unit lives, all lance allies on team get 2x SP.\n(Only highest value applied. Does not stack.)
MSID_H_斧の技量1: While unit lives and uses an axe, unit gets\n1.5x SP. (Only highest value applied. Does\nnot stack.)
MSID_H_斧の技量2: While unit lives, all axe allies on team get 1.5x SP.\n(Only highest value applied. Does not stack.)
MSID_H_斧の技量3: While unit lives, all axe allies on team get 2x SP.\n(Only highest value applied. Does not stack.)

MSID_H_翼槍ヴィドフニル: If foe initiates combat and uses sword, lance, or\naxe, grants Def+7 during combat.
MSID_H_魔性の槍: Accelerates Special trigger (cooldown count-1).\nGrants Atk/Spd+2. Deals 4 damage to unit after\ncombat.
MSID_H_キラーアクス2: Accelerates Special trigger\n(cooldown count-1).
MSID_H_キラーアクス2＋: Accelerates Special trigger\n(cooldown count-1).
MSID_H_蛇弓ニーズヘッグ: Effective against flying foes. During combat,\nboosts unit's Atk/Spd/Def/Res by number of\nadjacent allies × 2.
MSID_H_速さ守備1: Grants Spd/Def+1.
MSID_H_速さ守備2: Grants Spd/Def+2.
MSID_H_魔防の城塞1: Grants Res+3.\nInflicts Atk-3.
MSID_H_魔防の城塞2: Grants Res+4.\nInflicts Atk-3.
MSID_H_魔防の城塞3: Grants Res+5.\nInflicts Atk-3.
MSID_H_攻撃守備封じ1: Inflicts Atk/Def-3 on foe through its next action\nafter combat.
MSID_H_攻撃守備封じ2: Inflicts Atk/Def-5 on foe through its next action\nafter combat.
MSID_H_重装の行軍1: At start of turn, if unit's HP = 100% and unit is\nadjacent to an armored ally, unit and adjacent\narmored allies can move 1 extra space. (That turn\nonly. Does not stack.)
MSID_H_重装の行軍2: At start of turn, if unit's HP ≥ 50% and unit is\nadjacent to an armored ally, unit and adjacent\narmored allies can move 1 extra space. (That turn\nonly. Does not stack.)
MSID_H_重装の行軍3: At start of turn, if unit is adjacent to an armored\nally, unit and adjacent armored allies can move\n1 extra space. (That turn only. Does not stack.)
MSID_H_空からの先導1: If unit's HP = 100%, infantry and armored allies\nwithin 2 spaces can move to a space adjacent to\nunit.
MSID_H_空からの先導2: If unit's HP ≥ 50%, infantry and armored allies\nwithin 2 spaces can move to a space adjacent to\nunit.
MSID_H_空からの先導3: Infantry and armored allies within 2 spaces\ncan move to a space adjacent to unit.

MSID_H_聖剣ティルフィング: Grants Res+3. Reduces damage from magic foe's\nfirst attack by 50%.
MSID_H_瞬閃アイラの剣: Grants Spd+3. If unit's Spd > foe's Spd, grants\nSpecial cooldown charge +1 per attack. (Only\nhighest value applied. Does not stack.)
MSID_H_ファラフレイム: At start of turn, inflicts Atk/Res-4 on foes in\ncardinal directions with Res < unit's Res through\ntheir next actions.
MSID_H_聖書ナーガ: Effective against dragon foes. Neutralizes foe's\nbonuses (from skills like Fortify, Rally, etc.) during\ncombat.
MSID_H_速さ魔防の応援: Grants Spd/Res+3 to target ally for 1 turn.
MSID_H_剣姫の流星: Boosts damage dealt by 40% of unit's Spd.\n(Skill cannot be inherited.)
MSID_H_聖騎士の加護: If unit receives consecutive attacks and foe's\nRange = 2, reduces damage from foe's second\nattack onward by 80%. (Skill cannot be inherited.)
MSID_H_追撃リング: At start of combat, if unit's HP ≥ 50%, unit makes\na guaranteed follow-up attack. (Skill cannot be\ninherited.)
MSID_H_リカバーリング: At start of turn, restores 10 HP. (Skill cannot be\ninherited.)
MSID_H_速さの紫煙1: Inflicts Spd-3 on foes within 2 spaces of target\nthrough their next actions after combat.
MSID_H_速さの紫煙2: Inflicts Spd-5 on foes within 2 spaces of target\nthrough their next actions after combat.
MSID_H_速さの紫煙3: Inflicts Spd-7 on foes within 2 spaces of target\nthrough their next actions after combat.
MSID_H_速さの謀策1: At start of turn, inflicts Spd-3 on foes in cardinal\ndirections with Res < unit’s Res through their next\nactions.
MSID_H_速さの謀策2: At start of turn, inflicts Spd-4 on foes in cardinal\ndirections with Res < unit’s Res through their next\nactions.
MSID_H_速さの謀策3: At start of turn, inflicts Spd-5 on foes in cardinal\ndirections with Res < unit’s Res through their next\nactions.

MSID_H_クライネの弓: Effective against flying foes. If unit initiates\ncombat, inflicts Atk/Spd-5 on foes within 2 spaces\nof target through their next actions after combat.
MSID_H_クライネの弓＋: Effective against flying foes. If unit initiates\ncombat, inflicts Atk/Spd-5 on foes within 2 spaces\nof target through their next actions after combat.
MSID_H_ラウアアウル: During combat, boosts unit's Atk/Spd/Def/Res by\nnumber of adjacent allies × 2.
MSID_H_ラウアアウル＋: During combat, boosts unit's Atk/Spd/Def/Res by\nnumber of adjacent allies × 2.
MSID_H_守備魔防の応援: Grants Def/Res+3 to target ally for 1 turn.
MSID_H_鬼神金剛の一撃1: If unit initiates combat, grants Atk/Def+2 during\ncombat.
MSID_H_鬼神金剛の一撃2: If unit initiates combat, grants Atk/Def+4 during\ncombat.
MSID_H_生命の業火1: At start of combat, if unit’s HP ≥ foe's HP+3,\ngrants Atk+2 during combat.
MSID_H_生命の業火2: At start of combat, if unit’s HP ≥ foe's HP+3,\ngrants Atk+4 during combat.
MSID_H_生命の業火3: At start of combat, if unit’s HP ≥ foe's HP+3,\ngrants Atk+6 during combat.
MSID_H_守備の大紋章1: Grants Def+2 to allies within 2 spaces during\ncombat.
MSID_H_守備の大紋章2: Grants Def+3 to allies within 2 spaces during\ncombat.
MSID_H_攻撃の謀策1: At start of turn, inflicts Atk-3 on foes in cardinal\ndirections with Res < unit’s Res through their next\nactions.
MSID_H_攻撃の謀策2: At start of turn, inflicts Atk-4 on foes in cardinal\ndirections with Res < unit’s Res through their next\nactions.
MSID_H_攻撃の謀策3: At start of turn, inflicts Atk-5 on foes in cardinal\ndirections with Res < unit’s Res through their next\nactions.
MSID_H_恐慌の奇策1: At start of turn, converts bonuses on foes in\ncardinal directions with HP ≤ unit's HP-5 into\npenalties through their next actions.
MSID_H_恐慌の奇策2: At start of turn, converts bonuses on foes in\ncardinal directions with HP ≤ unit's HP-3 into\npenalties through their next actions.
MSID_H_恐慌の奇策3: At start of turn, converts bonuses on foes in\ncardinal directions with HP < unit's HP into\npenalties through their next actions.
MSID_H_剣の経験1: While unit lives and uses a sword, unit gets\n1.5x EXP. (Only highest value applied. Does not\nstack.)
MSID_H_剣の経験2: While unit lives, all sword allies on team get\n1.5x EXP. (Only highest value applied. Does not\nstack.)
MSID_H_剣の経験3: While unit lives, all sword allies on team get\n2x EXP. (Only highest value applied. Does not\nstack.)

MSID_H_ベオクの加護: Neutralizes cavalry and flying foes’ bonuses (from\nskills like Fortify, Rally, etc.) during combat. (Skill\ncannot be inherited.)
MSID_H_サカの加護: If foe uses sword, lance, or axe, foe cannot\ncounterattack. (Skill cannot be inherited.)

MPID_H_ルーテ: A young mage of Renais with an unusual\ntemperament. Confident in her abilities.\nAppears in Fire Emblem: The Sacred Stones.
MPID_H_ワユ: A mercenary fighting to improve her sword\nskills. In life, she doesn't sweat the details.\nAppears in Fire Emblem: Path of Radiance.

MSID_H_気鋭ワユの剣: Grants Atk+3. Deals +10 damage when Special\ntriggers.
MSID_H_氷剣アウドムラ: Accelerates Special trigger (cooldown count-1).\nGrants Res+5.
MSID_H_剛斧トマホーク: Unit can counterattack regardless of foe's range.
MSID_H_奇異ルーテの書: Grants Spd+3. At start of turn, inflicts Spd-5 on\nfoes in cardinal directions with Res < unit’s Res\nthrough their next actions.
MSID_H_HP魔防1: Grants HP+3, Res+1.
MSID_H_HP魔防2: Grants HP+4, Res+2.
MSID_H_鬼神の構え1: If foe initiates combat, grants Atk+2 during\ncombat.
MSID_H_鬼神の構え2: If foe initiates combat, grants Atk+4 during\ncombat.
MSID_H_鬼神の構え3: If foe initiates combat, grants Atk+6 during\ncombat.
MSID_H_柔剣1: If unit’s Spd ≥ foe’s Spd+5, grants Special\ncooldown charge +1 per attack. (Only highest\nvalue applied. Does not stack.)
MSID_H_柔剣2: If unit’s Spd ≥ foe’s Spd+3, grants Special\ncooldown charge +1 per attack. (Only highest\nvalue applied. Does not stack.)
MSID_H_柔剣3: If unit’s Spd > foe’s Spd, grants Special\ncooldown charge +1 per attack. (Only highest\nvalue applied. Does not stack.)
